  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0bc58a64-90fd-4dea-be4e-f81ae07300ce'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer9942352474448921988">Don't miss this breathtaking collection of stories set in the world of the New York Times best-selling Darkest Minds trilogy. Featuring ebook original novellas <i>In Time</i> and <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and a gripping, brand-new novella, <i>Through the Dark</i> is a must-have for fans of the Darkest Minds. This collection contains three novellas: <i>In Time</i>, <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and <i>Beyond the Night</i>, as well</span>
  <span id="freeText9942352474448921988" style="display:none">Don't miss this breathtaking collection of stories set in the world of the New York Times best-selling Darkest Minds trilogy. Featuring ebook original novellas <i>In Time</i> and <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and a gripping, brand-new novella, <i>Through the Dark</i> is a must-have for fans of the Darkest Minds. This collection contains three novellas: <i>In Time</i>, <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and <i>Beyond the Night</i>, as well as a sneak peek at the first novel in Alexandra Bracken's new series, <i>Passenger</i>. <br /><br />IN TIME <br />Gabe's life has been devastated in the wake of the economic crash. The only option left for someone like him to escape his tragic past is to leave his small town behind and to attempt to become a skiptracer. This already almost-impossible task is made all the more difficult by his first "score,"a young girl who won't speak, but who changes his life in ways he could never imagine. <br /><br />SPARKS RISE <br />Sam didn't think things could get worse at Thurmand rehabilitation camp. Then the Reds arrive. Everyone assumed the kids with firepower had been killed years ago. Instead they were taken away, brainwashed, and returned as terrifyingly effective guards. To her horror, Sam recognizes one of them: Lucas, the one spark of light in Sam's dark childhood. Lucas has a deadly secret--he beat the brutal training that turned his fellow Reds into mindless drones. When Sam defends herself against an attack by a vile PSF guard and faces a harrowing punishment, Lucas must risk everything to save her. <br /><br />BEYOND THE NIGHT <br />The government-run "rehabilitation camps" have been shut down, but kids with Psi powers are anything but free. Sam would rather be on her own than put in the care of a foster family and given the "cure"--a dangerous procedure that unclaimed kids across the country are being forced to undergo. But there's more at stake than just her own safety. Sam once made someone a promise, and the time has come to fulfill it. Now that she's out of her camp, Mia only has one thought in her head: finding Lucas, her beloved older brother.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9942352474448921988" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

<div id="review_1275803714" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1275803714" />
    <a title="Emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35715441-emma"><img alt="Emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446584145p2/35715441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1275803714?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma" href="/user/show/35715441-emma">Emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35715441-emma?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1275803714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3037102909681752424">Oh god. WHAT. A. BOOK. I cried A LOT. Even if these novellas aren't that long, they are just perfect and I was an emotional wreck, believe me. Every novella was pure gold and the new characters are so unique and different. I can't help but admire Bracken's writing style. <br/><br/>I was SCREAMING when out of no where MY SWEET BBY LIAM CAME BACK. (Okay, I think I was screaming AND sobbing.) He is such a sweetheart and this book just made me love him even more if that's even possible. I hadn't even realized</span>
  <span id="freeText3037102909681752424" style="display:none">Oh god. WHAT. A. BOOK. I cried A LOT. Even if these novellas aren't that long, they are just perfect and I was an emotional wreck, believe me. Every novella was pure gold and the new characters are so unique and different. I can't help but admire Bracken's writing style. <br /><br />I was SCREAMING when out of no where MY SWEET BBY LIAM CAME BACK. (Okay, I think I was screaming AND sobbing.) He is such a sweetheart and this book just made me love him even more if that's even possible. I hadn't even realized how much I had missed my favorite group! AHHHHHHHHHH I don't want to let go of these wonderful characters again! Nooooooo!<br /><br /><b>Mild spoilers ahead,</b> so if you have not read this book yet, GO READ IT. You will NOT be disappointed!!<br /><br />5<br />4<br />3<br />2<br />1<br /><br />Alright then! Let's start!<br /><br /><b>IN TIME:</b> I knew what would happen. I was so certain of it, but still I tried to deny it and have my hopes up. "Maybe this time it'll be different...." I whispered to myself. And then.... <b>BOOOOOM.</b> Alexandra Bracken just shot an arrow right through my heart. *ugly sobbing*<br /><br /><b>SPARKS RISE:</b> New characters! Yay! I absolutely loved this novella. Our new characters, Sam and Lucas are BRILLIANT. But the more I read, the more I started to fear. "Okay, this <i>has</i> to end well. There's <i>no way</i> this'll end like In Time. [insert fearful laugh] There just <i>can't be</i> another heartbreaking novella after another, right? ...Right?" And guess what? <b>BOOOOOOOM.</b> Now there were two arrows sticking out of my heart. *ugly sobbing continued as my hopes died*<br /><br /><b> BEYOND THE NIGHT:</b> This was probably my favorite novella! The old squad is BACK. And like I said earlier, my mind (and heart) went ASDFGHJJGFDSSDF when I realized my babies were included in this story! A new character, Mia, was fantastic. I loved this new trio's dynamic and if you mix the old gang and the new trio together - perfection. This was really an emotional roller coaster for me. The ending was amazing and it does hurt a bit to leave these characters behind <i>again. </i> *sigh*<br /><br />5/5 stars. I regret nothing. Go read this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3037102909681752424" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1993914036" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1993914036" />
    <a title="Katie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18469518-katie"><img alt="Katie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1492999493p2/18469518.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1993914036?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie" href="/user/show/18469518-katie">Katie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26873299-through-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18469518-katie?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18469518-katie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18469518-katie?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18469518-katie?shelf=4-star-rating">4-star-rating</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1993914036" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15924325378572904957">I really enjoyed this collection of novellas! I liked that we got to see some different perspectives during The Darkest Minds (but away from Ruby and the main story), as well as seeing how the world was changing and adapting after the last book ended.<br/><br/>While I liked In Time, Sparks Rise and Beyond the Night are what really made this book worth it. I felt that while it was nice getting Gabe's perspective in In Time, which was so drastically different as he was not one of the kids with powers, he wa</span>
  <span id="freeText15924325378572904957" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this collection of novellas! I liked that we got to see some different perspectives during The Darkest Minds (but away from Ruby and the main story), as well as seeing how the world was changing and adapting after the last book ended.<br /><br />While I liked In Time, Sparks Rise and Beyond the Night are what really made this book worth it. I felt that while it was nice getting Gabe's perspective in In Time, which was so drastically different as he was not one of the kids with powers, he wasn't really likable for most of the novella. I think that was the point, to see him grow and change, but this was the shortest of the novellas and I think it was a disservice because everything happened too quickly to really care about what happened to him.<br /><br />Sparks Rise and Beyond the Night were both told in alternating POVs (Sparks Rise was Sam and her friend Lucas and Beyond the Night was Sam and Mia, Lucas's sister). In Sparks Rise, we saw more of the brutality of Thurmond, which obviously wasn't enjoyable, but I liked seeing more of the camp to really drive home how horrible these camps were. And Beyond the Night takes place after the events of In the Afterlight, and I loved getting to see the gang again, although it was really interesting seeing them from a different perspective. <br /><br />I wish Beyond the Night was split into more than 5 chapters. I understand that it was done to flip back and forth between Sam and Mia, but I wish each of them was separated into parts because the chapters were super long (and I like short chapters lol). Also, I wish that I had read this right after I finished In the Afterlight. I still enjoyed this a lot, but it would have been better if the events of the trilogy were fresher in my mind.<br /><br />Definitely recommend for people who like The Darkest Minds trilogy - especially because of Beyond the Night, which wraps up some lingering questions from the end of In the Afterlight.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15924325378572904957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1284490887" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1284490887" />
    <a title="Pinky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27523984-pinky"><img alt="Pinky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489855494p2/27523984.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1284490887?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pinky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pinky" href="/user/show/27523984-pinky">Pinky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27523984-pinky?shelf=books-i-want-to-own">books-i-want-to-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1284490887" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3937522354390441106"> When I heard that this book came out, I wanted to get it so badly. I haven't finished Winter, which is part of yet another series I love. And I haven't got the chance to read The Stolen Chapters, my most anticipated read of 2016! There are so many books but so little time. I really want to catch up because I am scared I am going to be spoiled and I want to discuss the books with others.<br/><br/>Everyone talks about all of these books and I want to join in because...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455246772ra/18078016.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“We will move forward as one, and i</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText3937522354390441106" style="display:none"> When I heard that this book came out, I wanted to get it so badly. I haven't finished Winter, which is part of yet another series I love. And I haven't got the chance to read The Stolen Chapters, my most anticipated read of 2016! There are so many books but so little time. I really want to catch up because I am scared I am going to be spoiled and I want to discuss the books with others.<br><br>Everyone talks about all of these books and I want to join in because...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455246772ra/18078016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“We will move forward as one, and in time, rise like sparks beyond the night.” </b>
</i><br> <br> I am so glad I got the chance to read this book, it was a great way to return to another beautiful world that I love. It was a great experience, and it is a really good read. But, this is a bunch of nouvellas for the Darkest Minds Trilogy. <br><br> If you haven't heard of the Darkest Minds Trilogy, it is basically about a girl named Ruby who was locked in her basement on her 10th birthday. Her parents believed that she was acting strange and a bunch of soldiers showed up at her house and took her away into a camp. This camp had a bunch of other kids who were all sorted into different colors. These colors represented a certain ability that each kid had. Kids were either Green, Red, Orange, Yellow or Blue. This camp isn't one of those fun summer camps, it was more of the type of camp where you might die any second if you make the wrong move. In order to survive, Ruby feels the need to escape and after this, her adventure will begin.<br><br> I don't know if that was the best summary because it's been a while since I read the series. I remember that it was really good so I highly recommend it if you haven't read it already. If you have read the series, I highly recommend you read this because you are missing out! It was an amazing experience and we got more from the world. We saw from different points of view that we haven't seen before and we learn more about the characters.<br><br>When I read about the characters, I was like,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455246772ra/18078017.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> It was interesting to see how different characters survive or attempt to survive. Most of the nouvellas had me crying because of how sad they were, the suffering and pain hits you hard in the feels. But it was all worth it, we get to see the characters from the Darkest Minds trilogy and it made up for all of the sad parts.<br><br>Even though it can be sad...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455246772ra/18078018.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Right when I started reading, I couldn't stop, it was fast paced and it was hard to put the book down. Once again, I highly recommend you read this! It was really good and you will be glad that you did! Trust me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455246772ra/18078019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3937522354390441106" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1448101153" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1448101153" />
    <a title="Theresa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7822909-theresa"><img alt="Theresa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579483036p2/7822909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1448101153?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Theresa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Theresa" href="/user/show/7822909-theresa">Theresa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1448101153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10324639809618250650">Alexandra Bracken is legit my favorite author. She is so talented and can I please just BE HER. Her characters are phenomenal and her descriptions and style are amazing. She can create such a fleshed out and colorful world for her readers that is really incredible. She is an amazing story teller. These novellas were so great, and this world she created for TDM has been expanded perfectly. Anyone who read TDM series should pick this book up, it is so so great. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18284197759385090704"><b> actual rating: 4.5/5</b> <br/><br/><br/><b>We will move forward as one, and in time, rise like sparks beyond the night. </b><br/><br/>I have been a huge fan of the darkest minds series since i first started reading them and i have always felt like i needed some more closure and i feel like this book gave me that closure i needed. <br/><br/>Following Gabe's story in the first one was a really great story to start off with because it's about change and he makes some throughout the novella and even more so when he meets the little girl who do</span>
  <span id="freeText18284197759385090704" style="display:none"><b> actual rating: 4.5/5</b> <br /><br /><br /><b>We will move forward as one, and in time, rise like sparks beyond the night. </b><br /><br />I have been a huge fan of the darkest minds series since i first started reading them and i have always felt like i needed some more closure and i feel like this book gave me that closure i needed. <br /><br />Following Gabe's story in the first one was a really great story to start off with because it's about change and he makes some throughout the novella and even more so when he meets the little girl who doesn't speak. <br /><br />I really loved getting the last two novella's about sam and how she was after Ruby escaped from the camp. I feel like i got the much needed closure on what happened with Sam after Ruby and how she dealt with things during that time and i finally got the answers that i had been wanting. <br /><br /><b>Home isn’t four walls, it’s the people you’re with. </b><br /><br />I can say that i was extremely satisfied with how this novella played out and i cannot wait to start book four knowing what i know now from reading this one. </span>

<div id="review_3456609580" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3456609580" />
    <a title="❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl"><img alt="❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580347605p2/104675816.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3456609580?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl)" href="/user/show/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl">❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781368022484" href="/book/show/35099467-through-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ❀ Alex ❀ (The Scribe Owl) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/112791757-kat-blackwood">Kat Blackwood</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl?shelf=post-apocalyptic">post-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104675816-alex-the-scribe-owl?shelf=novella">novella</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3456609580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3214019883767782702">Come see this review and more at my blog, <a href='thescribeowl.wordpress.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Scribe Owl!</a><br/><br/><i>Thanks to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/112791757-kat-blackwood' rel='nofollow noopener'> Kat Blackwood </a> for a copy of the K to finish the DARK on my shelf!</i><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_' title='The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Minds</a>: ★★★★★<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_' title='Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>Never Fade</a>: ★★★★☆<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150831.In_The_Afterlight__The_Darkest_Minds___3_' title='In The Afterlight (The Darkest Minds, #3) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>In The Afterlight</a>: ★★★½☆<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25453426.Through_the_Dark__The_Darkest_Minds___1_5___2_5___3_5_' title='Through the Dark (The Darkest Minds, #1.5, #2.5, #3.5) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>Through the Dark</a>: ★★★★☆<br/><br/>Wow. I wasn't expecting much from this because novellas are never quite as good as the books in the actual series, but this one fits in perfectly. In my opinion, it even beat In the Afterlight! I'm so glad I enjoyed this against all odds. Happy accidents!<br/><br/><b>In Time (1.5): ★★★★☆</b><br/>The</span>
  <span id="freeText3214019883767782702" style="display:none">Come see this review and more at my blog, <a href="thescribeowl.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">The Scribe Owl!</a><br /><br /><i>Thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/112791757-kat-blackwood" rel="nofollow noopener"> Kat Blackwood </a> for a copy of the K to finish the DARK on my shelf!</i><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_" title="The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Minds</a>: ★★★★★<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_" title="Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Fade</a>: ★★★★☆<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150831.In_The_Afterlight__The_Darkest_Minds___3_" title="In The Afterlight (The Darkest Minds, #3) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">In The Afterlight</a>: ★★★½☆<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25453426.Through_the_Dark__The_Darkest_Minds___1_5___2_5___3_5_" title="Through the Dark (The Darkest Minds, #1.5, #2.5, #3.5) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Dark</a>: ★★★★☆<br /><br />Wow. I wasn't expecting much from this because novellas are never quite as good as the books in the actual series, but this one fits in perfectly. In my opinion, it even beat In the Afterlight! I'm so glad I enjoyed this against all odds. Happy accidents!<br /><br /><b>In Time (1.5): ★★★★☆</b><br />The first novella took place after The Darkest Minds and before Neverfade when Zu was traveling to her family in California. We saw her meet Gabe, who wanted to turn her in for the reward. We get to see his mind slowly change because let's face it Zu is an angel. This was the shortest one, so I didn't get to learn our new character of Gabe that well, but when stuff went down it the end, oh it hurt. It <i>hurt.</i> I never knew how badly I needed those happy endings until they were taken away.<br /><br /><b>Sparks Rise (2.5): ★★★★★</b><br />Sparks Rise was my absolute favorite. We got to look into the life of Sam, Ruby's best friend from Thurmond, and see what the camp were like after Ruby left. This one takes place right between Neverfade and In the Afterlight. Sam meets her best friend from before they was taken by the PSFs, Lucas Orfeo. And Lucas is a Red. But somehow his mind isn't fractured like the others', and he and Sam devise a plan to escape. The ending here hurt too. Hurt more, to be honest, because we had more time to meet the characters. I won't even start to talk about, because then I know I'm done for. <br /><br /><b>Beyond the Night (3.5): ★★★★☆</b><br />Beyond the Night was like a 200 page long epilogue to In the Afterlight. Most of the loose ends from the third book were tied up neatly, leaving just enough for Zu's new book, The Darkest Legacy. Beyond the Night was told in the perspectives of Sam and Mia, Lucas's sister, though we had Ruby, Lee, Vi, and Chubs make a length appearance. It was so fantastic to see the gang again, and it was a relief to have the ending of Sparks rise cleaned up.<br /><br /><b>Overall</b><br />All in all, I'm so glad I was gifted a copy of this book. I never knew I needed it until I finished it! I would definitely recommend it. While not essential to understanding the rest of the series, it will definitely make your read more enjoyable. <br /><br />Trigger and content warnings: Blood, death, loss of a loved one, attempted rape, and violence. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3214019883767782702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2672499164573616298">4.5 AMAZING stars! I'm not usually a huge fan of novellas because I typically only ever want more of my favorite characters/what happens in the future, not the last. But these novellas were beyond perfect! <br/><br/>In Time was my least favorite, but still heart breakingly touching. <br/><br/>Sparks Rise was an incredible introduction to Lucas and I'm so happy we got to see more of Sam!   <span id="freeText2672499164573616298" style="display:none">4.5 AMAZING stars! I'm not usually a huge fan of novellas because I typically only ever want more of my favorite characters/what happens in the future, not the last. But these novellas were beyond perfect! <br /><br />In Time was my least favorite, but still heart breakingly touching. <br /><br />Sparks Rise was an incredible introduction to Lucas and I'm so happy we got to see more of Sam! But again, HEART BREAKING.<br /><br />Beyond the Night was absolute perfection! Seeing the old squad together again made my heart do a little happy dance. I laughed, I cried, and I didn't want it to end! I loved seeing what happened to Sam, Mia, and Lucas and I'm so happy so many of the questions I had at the end of In The Afterlight were answered. Still sobbing over Cole and drooling over Liam. <br /><br />Haven't read these yet? GO READ THEM NOW!</span>

<div id="review_1410336187" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1410336187" />
    <a title="Isabel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8613830-isabel"><img alt="Isabel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585583126p2/8613830.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1410336187?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isabel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isabel" href="/user/show/8613830-isabel">Isabel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1410336187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8220442152935068439">Wow.<br/><br/>Wow.<br/><br/>Honestly.<br/><br/>I had already read <i>In Time</i> (#1.5) and <i>Sparks Rise</i> (#2.5) before this, but wow. <i>Beyond the Night</i> (#3.5) is really something special.<br/><br/>I don't know how to make this review extra special but I feel like it needs to be. This series is so important to me and I love it so much, but this is the end and as much as that makes me sad, I'm also glad that it ended with <i>Beyond the Night</i>. It's closure, it's answered questions, and it wraps the series up nicely. <br/><br/>And sure, you can get away with j</span>
  <span id="freeText8220442152935068439" style="display:none">Wow.<br /><br />Wow.<br /><br />Honestly.<br /><br />I had already read <i>In Time</i> (#1.5) and <i>Sparks Rise</i> (#2.5) before this, but wow. <i>Beyond the Night</i> (#3.5) is really something special.<br /><br />I don't know how to make this review extra special but I feel like it needs to be. This series is so important to me and I love it so much, but this is the end and as much as that makes me sad, I'm also glad that it ended with <i>Beyond the Night</i>. It's closure, it's answered questions, and it wraps the series up nicely. <br /><br />And sure, you can get away with just reading <i>The Darkest Minds, Never Fade</i>, and <i>In the Afterlight</i>, but these "inbetweener" books add so much. There's a lot of questions about the world answered in these books, and a lot of other characters are explored. It's not like they each are a retelling of the three main books but from other character's perspectives, these are actual, individual characters narrating events as they happen. <br /><br />Also, be prepared to cry. Grab those tissues. Shut the door to your room and cry your eyes out. Happy or sad tears, it doesn't matter, anything is possible!<br /><br />I really wish I had more to say, or, more accurately, I wish I knew how to put my love into words. These characters are like family to me and I know that sounds <i>so</i> cheesy, but honestly they light up my day. Chubs and Vida are so funny, Liam and Ruby are just giant sweethearts, and Sam and Lucas have quickly earned their place on my list of favorite characters. Mia, of course, is not left out, as well as Zu. They're all so perfect and I want to make sure that my review is good and solid because this is the last book! <br /><br />(Is there an emoji for bawling my eyes out?)<br /><br />Five <i>hundred</i> stars out of five, and let me just say that I'm trying really hard to think of books that are similar to these, but I can't. <i>The Darkest Minds</i> is pretty much the book I base everything off of. <br /><br />I'm sorry, usually this is where I put, "If you liked [specific book], you'll like <i>Through the Dark</i> and the rest of the series," but I honestly can't think of a single book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8220442152935068439" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=novellas-and-short-stories">novellas-and-short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=favorite-covers">favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=gorgeous-writing">gorgeous-writing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417941434" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14926984973609471719"><i>Through The Dark: A Darkest Minds Collection</i> is the compilation of all the three novellas of The Darkest Minds series. It contains <i>In Time</i>, <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and the very exclusive to this bunch: <i>Beyond the Night</i>.<br/><br/>This collection is genius! In this book, we get to see different areas of struggles for different people in the world of The Darkest Minds. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>In Time</b>
</i><b></b><br/>I think <i>In Time</i> is really short. It focuses on the life of Gabe, a young man who aspires to be a skip-tracer, who met Zu, a yellow, along his</span>
  <span id="freeText14926984973609471719" style="display:none"><i>Through The Dark: A Darkest Minds Collection</i> is the compilation of all the three novellas of The Darkest Minds series. It contains <i>In Time</i>, <i>Sparks Rise</i>, and the very exclusive to this bunch: <i>Beyond the Night</i>.<br /><br />This collection is genius! In this book, we get to see different areas of struggles for different people in the world of The Darkest Minds. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>In Time</b>
</i><b></b><br />I think <i>In Time</i> is really short. It focuses on the life of Gabe, a young man who aspires to be a skip-tracer, who met Zu, a yellow, along his way to search for kids to turn in.<br /><br />What I can say was that Gabe is one of those characters that you would want to be in the main series. I think he’s one of those you would want to see developing and changing through time and getting somewhere bigger. It would have been good to see him with a greater purpose. So, I think this novella was too short for such a good character as him.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Sparks Rise</b>
</i><b></b><br />With Sam’s and Lucas’s alternate narrations, <i>Sparks Rise</i> takes place after Ruby escaped Thurmond. It is about Sam and what happened to her after being left in that place when the Reds were brought back into the camp after years of “programming” in the Project Jamboree which was mentioned somewhere in the parent series.<br /><br />Here’s what I think: Sam and Lucas deserve a full-length novel!!!! When I was reading this one, I was panicking inside. I was so excited for the two of them!<br /><br />I don’t know if it was just me being a cry-baby but the last two sentences of the last chapter narrated by Sam made me cry! How could two simple sentences make someone cry??? Those were everything! It was the bomb to my emotions!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Beyond the Night</b>
</i><b></b><br />Thank you so much, Alexandra Bracken, for this!<br /><br />Please take note that you should have read <i>Sparks Rise</i> and <i> In the Afterlight</i> before proceeding to this one. <i> Beyond the Night</i> is told both from Sam’s and Mia’s points of view.<br /><br />This story serves two purposes: a continuation of <i> Sparks Rise</i> and a fuller epilogue of <i> In the Afterlight</i> It is a must-read!<br /><br />Beyond the Night is set after the story of <i>In the AfterLight</i>. It focuses on what happened after the camps were taken down. This novella, that’s almost like a full-length novel because it’s pretty long, is like an extended and satisfying epilogue that wraps up the whole series. I love it so much because it has more of a closure for me. It’s not that I didn’t love the ending of the third book in its parent series; it’s just that this one has me like: “Okay, I can now depart from this world”, although I would gladly appreciate another book or novella in addition to this series.<br /><br />What to expect:<br />1.)	Cars<br />2.)	Fairytales<br />3.)	“snatchers” instead of skip tracers<br />4.)	Some burning<br />5.)	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ruby, Liam, Chubs, and Vida!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />6.)	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The issue on the Reds being resolved somewhat—if you didn’t notice it, it was sort of left hanging in the air by the end of the third book. In here, we get to see the start of a progress of helping the Reds recover.<br /><br />Although we get to see new hope for the Reds in this story, I think another novella or full-length novel that tackles this problem would be really good. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />7.)	A <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ HEA  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So, to sum this review up, all I can say is that you have to buy a copy of this bundle of good stuff and read it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14926984973609471719" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1427099066" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1427099066" />
    <a title="Alyssa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4152087-alyssa"><img alt="Alyssa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395375020p2/4152087.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1427099066?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/4152087-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1427099066" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13531589377872919312"><b>IN TIME</b> 3 stars<br/><br/>It’s been a long time since I’ve last been immersed in Bracken’s THE DARKEST MINDS, but I came back to this series like an old friend. This collection of novellas made me realize how much I missed her writing style and how easy it is to slip into the worlds she creates.<br/><br/>IN TIME introduces a funny, sort of sarcastic main character I can relate to. He can be a little annoying at first because he isn’t exactly off to do good things but CHARACTER DEVELOPMENT. It also added some humor, </span>
  <span id="freeText13531589377872919312" style="display:none"><b>IN TIME</b> 3 stars<br /><br />It’s been a long time since I’ve last been immersed in Bracken’s THE DARKEST MINDS, but I came back to this series like an old friend. This collection of novellas made me realize how much I missed her writing style and how easy it is to slip into the worlds she creates.<br /><br />IN TIME introduces a funny, sort of sarcastic main character I can relate to. He can be a little annoying at first because he isn’t exactly off to do good things but CHARACTER DEVELOPMENT. It also added some humor, which I loved!<br /><br />This one is made a lot more powerful if you have already read THE DARKEST MINDS because some familiar faces appear and the story comes off more meaningful. That being said, you don’t need to read the book first but it would greatly behoove you as this is technically book 1.5. The same goes for the rest of the novellas.<blockquote>“When you have nothing for so long, you forget the terror of having something to lose.”</blockquote> <b>SPARKS RISE</b> 4 stars<br /><br />Now I’m just wondering why all these novellas are so depressing! But I love it. This one hit me a little harder emotionally because I felt we got to know the characters so much more deeply than the ones in IN TIME. SPARKS RISE focuses more on the characters and less about what is going on around them, although that stuff is still relevant and important and leads to a conclusion that I NEED resolution on, stat!<br /><br />We spend a lot of time in the character’s heads seeing their wants and fears and dreams and personalities so I really connected to them and genuinely worried about them. SPARKS RISE made me feel ALL THE EMOTIONS. The cruelty Sam experienced was especially hard to read, the kids in these camps face both mental and physical pain and it made me want to gather them all together and make sure nothing ever happened to them.<blockquote>“Hell isn’t a place you go; Hell is where we live now. Hell is being helpless to protect the people you care about the most, and save them from themselves.</blockquote><b>BEYOND THE NIGHT</b> 4 stars<br /><br />Luckily, this one takes place after IN THE AFTERLIGHT, the final book in The Darkest Minds series and ties up some loose ends we might have had, including one major one from the last novella!<br /><br />It was really fun to see what our favorite characters are up to and how their stories intersect with those from SPARKS RISE. This one was not devoid of the FEELS either, the ending made me tear up-in a good way!<br /><br />Overall, I think this series of novellas really adds something to the story of these characters and the world they live in and would recommend adding it to your collection. <a href="http://readerswonderland.com/2015/10/review-through-the-dark-by-alexandra-bracken-giveaway/" rel="nofollow noopener">You’re in luck because we are giving away a copy courtesy of Disney-Hyperion!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13531589377872919312" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1372940706" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1372940706" />
    <a title="Chelsea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33012180-chelsea"><img alt="Chelsea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537582300p2/33012180.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1372940706?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea" href="/user/show/33012180-chelsea">Chelsea</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1372940706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15260926021965614047">I’m not exactly what you’d call a novella person. I read them very rarely, but I enjoy a novella bind up every once in a while. I’m not exactly Alexandra Bracken biggest fan, as while I enjoyed a lot of aspects from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_' title='The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Minds</a> I felt like the last two books in that series were pretty meh. <b>I do really love the world created within those books, and I think Bracken did a fantastic job exploring this brutal dystopian world through short stories.</b><br/><br/><b>In Time—4 ½ stars:</b> Damnnnnn… This novella was by</span>
  <span id="freeText15260926021965614047" style="display:none">I’m not exactly what you’d call a novella person. I read them very rarely, but I enjoy a novella bind up every once in a while. I’m not exactly Alexandra Bracken biggest fan, as while I enjoyed a lot of aspects from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_" title="The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Minds</a> I felt like the last two books in that series were pretty meh. <b>I do really love the world created within those books, and I think Bracken did a fantastic job exploring this brutal dystopian world through short stories.</b><br /><br /><b>In Time—4 ½ stars:</b> Damnnnnn… This novella was by far the best. I think I have a soft spot for this sort of story with the guy thrust into the role of reluctant caretaker of a child who he stubbornly tries to hate but ends up loving at the end. It’s just so freaking cute! This novella was both heartwarming and heartbreaking. The atmosphere was tense and felt very dystopian. The narrator’s voice was extremely well done and I felt very connected to him as a character through his voice.<br /><br /><b>Sparks Fly—3 stars:</b> Wasn’t a big fan of this one. I never really connected to Sam or Lucas, and the plot was very rape-y, which I guess would happen in this kind of world but I wasn’t sure how I felt about it being used in the plot as an opportunity for the love interest to come rescue Sam. Well written and all but I just didn’t enjoy this one in comparison to the first one. I did like the ending though.<br /><br /><b>Beyond The Night—4 stars:</b> Didn’t blow me away but I enjoyed it quite a bit! I liked Mia and getting to know Sam more, but honestly once all of the old characters turned up they just stole the show. I enjoyed this follow up although I would have preferred a follow up from the POV of the original characters.<br /><br /><b>Overall I would say this bind-up is well worth a read for fans of the series!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15260926021965614047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

	<tr>
		<td>
		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YEwc+YEKrsLiCjY9hqNTjO+YaGLKAmsJJ2lehdY5YweWl4uYg8zdA+VliVuvLBiB/Hu7pBqsBRC2QWcuJgr5qA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GaK7RYt9SwrnRkT/746VicvwacIVhHYDMpaVwm/egF7veSwkibs4y+Ap+5nGAd6E2BO6BMUqGBqjvqxpn+0a8Q==')})
  }
